Description: Controlled vocabulary of families
File name:   cv_family.txt
Last update: 25-Nov-2022

----------------------------------------------------------------------------

 The definition of the CV is provided in the following format:

 ---------  ---------------------------     ----------------------
 Line code  Content                         Occurrence in an entry
 ---------  ---------------------------     ----------------------
 ID         Identifier (family name)        Once; starts an entry
 AC         Accession (FA-xxxxx)            Once
 SY         Synonyms                        Optional; once or more
 DR         Xref on classification          Optional; once or more
 HI         Hierarchy                       Optional; once
 //         Terminator                      Once; ends an entry

AN   Next free AC: FA-05615
